**Fetch Alternatives**
----
	Returns json data in form of AlternativeResponse object which contains list of companies, historical performance data, simulation portfolios for the list of isins, portfolioId and esgTargetType passed as input.
*   **URL:**
    /alternative-service/alternatives
*   **Method:**
    `POST`
*   **Path Params:**
    _None_
*   **Required:**
    * **requestBody:**
	```json
	{
	  "esgTargetType": "string",
	  "isin": [
		"string"
	  ],
	  "portfolioId": "string"
	}
	```
*   **Data Params:**
    _None_
*   **Sample:**
    /alternative-service/alternatives
	* **requestBody:**
	```json
	{
	  "esgTargetType": "ESG",
	  "isin": [
		"US79466L3024", "US1667641005"
	  ],
	  "portfolioId": "1"
	}	
	```
*   **Success Response:**
    * **Code:** 200 <br />
    * **Content:** 
    ```json
    {

		"alternativeId" : 1,
    ```
